## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S
SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
BATCH_SIZE = 32768
IN_FEATURES = 1024
OUT_FEATURES = 4096
NUM_GROUPS = 64
GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
EPS = 1e-05

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
            x = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
                x += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)
            x += S.convert(BIAS0[j], S.f32)
            x = x / (one + S.exp(-x))
            x += S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[j], S.f32)
            Y[i, j] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                d = S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean
                var += d * d
            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

class ModelNew(nn.Module):

    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, bias_shape):
        super().__init__()
        self.matmul = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.bias = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(bias_shape))
        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or tuple(self.bias.shape) != (OUT_FEATURES,) or (self.group_norm.num_groups != NUM_GROUPS) or (self.group_norm.eps != EPS):
            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
        w_t = self.matmul.weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        bias0 = self.matmul.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        extra_bias = self.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x.contiguous(), w_t, bias0, extra_bias, gn_w, gn_b, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S
SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
BATCH_SIZE = 32768
IN_FEATURES = 1024
OUT_FEATURES = 4096
NUM_GROUPS = 64
GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
EPS = 1e-05

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
            x = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
                x += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)
            x += S.convert(BIAS0[j], S.f32)
            x = x / (one + S.exp(-x))
            x += S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[j], S.f32)
            Y[i, j] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                d = S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean
                var += d * d
            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):

                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)

        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_basic(
    input_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.i32),
    output_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.i32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((32,), S.i32)

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_buf[thread_id] = input_data[thread_id]

    S.syncthreads()

    read_idx = (thread_id + 1) % 32
    output_data[thread_id] = shared_buf[read_idx]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_2d(
    input_matrix: S.Tensor((16, 16), S.f32),
    output_matrix: S.Tensor((16, 16), S.f32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((16, 16), S.f32)

    thread_x = S.thread_id(0)
    thread_y = S.thread_id(1)

    shared_buf[thread_y, thread_x] = input_matrix[thread_y, thread_x]

    S.syncthreads()

    output_matrix[thread_y, thread_x] = shared_buf[thread_x, thread_y]  # Transpose


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_reduction(
    input_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.f32),
    result: S.Tensor((2,), S.f32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((32,), S.f32)

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_buf[thread_id] = input_data[thread_id]
    S.syncthreads()

    stride = 16
    for i in S.range(5):  # log2(32) = 5
        if thread_id < stride:
            shared_buf[thread_id] = shared_buf[thread_id] + shared_buf[thread_id + stride]
        S.syncthreads()
        stride = stride >> 0x1

    if thread_id == 0:
        result[0] = shared_buf[0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_offsets(result: S.Tensor((2,), S.u32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((16,), S.u32)
    left_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    right_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    layout = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    left = S.view(left_words, S.u32, layout)
    right = S.view(right_words, S.u32, layout)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        left[0, 0] = S.convert(11, S.u32)
        right[0, 0] = S.convert(22, S.u32)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = left[0, 0]
        result[1] = right[0, 0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_mixed_types(result: S.Tensor((4,), S.i32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((32,), S.u32)
    stats_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    q_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    kv_words = S.subview(shared_words, (16,), (8,), (1,))
    score_words = S.subview(shared_words, (24,), (8,), (1,))
    layout_f32 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_bf16 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_u32 = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    stats = S.view(stats_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q = S.view(q_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    kv = S.view(kv_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    score = S.view(score_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q_u32 = S.view(q_words, S.u32, layout_u32)
    kv_u32 = S.view(kv_words, S.u32, layout_u32)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        stats[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.f32)
        score[0, 0] = S.convert(4.0, S.f32)
        q[0, 0] = S.convert(1.0, S.bf16)
        q[0, 1] = S.convert(2.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 1] = S.convert(4.0, S.bf16)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = S.convert(stats[0, 0], S.i32)
        result[1] = q_u32[0, 0]
        result[2] = kv_u32[0, 0]
        result[3] = S.convert(score[0, 0], S.i32)


class TestSharedMemoryOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_basic_shared_memory(self):
        """Test basic shared memory read/write functionality"""
        input_data = torch.arange(32, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        output_data = torch.zeros(32, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        expected = torch.cat([input_data[1:], input_data[0:1]])

        kernel_shm_basic[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](input_data, output_data)

        actual = output_data.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_2d_shared_memory(self):
        """Test 2D shared memory with matrix transpose"""
        input_matrix = torch.arange(256, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda").reshape(16, 16)
        output_matrix = torch.zeros((16, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        expected = input_matrix.t()  # Transpose

        kernel_shm_2d[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (16, 16, 1))](input_matrix, output_matrix)

        actual = output_matrix.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(actual, expected),
            f"Max difference: {(actual - expected).abs().max()}",
        )

    def test_shm_reduction(self):
        """Test shared memory reduction operation"""
        input_data = torch.ones(32, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
        result = torch.zeros(2, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        expected = torch.sum(input_data)

        kernel_shm_reduction[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](input_data, result)

        actual = result[0].cpu().item()
        expected = expected.cpu().item()

        self.assertAlmostEqual(actual, expected, places=5, msg=f"Expected: {expected}, Got: {actual}")

    def test_shm_subview_view_offsets(self):
        """Test that typed views preserve non-zero shared subview offsets."""
        result = torch.zeros(2, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_shm_subview_view_offsets[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](result)

        actual = result.cpu()
        expected = torch.tensor([11, 22], dtype=torch.int32)

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_shm_subview_view_mixed_types(self):
        """Test mixed f32/bf16/u32 typed views on distinct shared subviews."""
        result = torch.zeros(4, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_shm_subview_view_mixed_types[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](result)

        actual = result.cpu()
        expected = torch.tensor([3, 1073758080, 1082146880, 4], dtype=torch.int32)

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

import torch
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32), B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32), C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32)):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)
    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    C[lane] = c_lane

def pack(rows):
    # rows: (64,4) bf16 values per lane
    x = rows.view(torch.uint16).reshape(64,4).to(torch.int32)
    lo = x[:,0] | (x[:,1] << 16)
    hi = x[:,2] | (x[:,3] << 16)
    return torch.stack([lo,hi], dim=1).to(torch.uint32)

# Try identity-like single active values to infer mapping.
# Build lane fragments corresponding to conceptual rows/cols maybe direct natural order.
A_frag = torch.zeros((64,4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
B_frag = torch.zeros((64,4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
# Activate first element in every lane
A_frag[:,0] = 1
B_frag[:,0] = 1
A = pack(A_frag)
B = pack(B_frag)
C = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')

import importlib.util, sys, torch
path='/workspace/substrate/test/examples/gemm/amdgpu/test_gemm_mfma.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mfma_mod', path)
mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
sys.modules['mfma_mod']=mod
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def pack(rows):
    x = rows.view(torch.uint16).reshape(64,4).to(torch.int32)
    lo = x[:,0] | (x[:,1] << 16)
    hi = x[:,2] | (x[:,3] << 16)
    return torch.stack([lo,hi], dim=1).to(torch.uint32)

def run_basis(r,k,c):
    A_frag = torch.zeros((64,4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    B_frag = torch.zeros((64,4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    a_lane = r*2 + (k//4)
    a_pos = k%4
    b_lane = k*8 + (c//4)
    b_pos = c%4
    A_frag[a_lane, a_pos] = 1
    B_frag[b_lane, b_pos] = 1
    A = pack(A_frag)
    B = pack(B_frag)
    C = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    mod.gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](A,B,C)
    nz = (C.cpu() "'!= 0).nonzero(as_tuple=False)
    vals = C.cpu()[C.cpu()!=0]
    print('"'basis', r,k,c, 'nz_count', nz.shape[0], 'first', nz[:20].tolist(), vals[:20].tolist())

for args in [(0,0,0),(0,0,1),(0,0,4),(1,0,0),(0,1,0),(0,4,0),(31,7,31)]:
    run_basis(*args)

+def _gemm_launch():

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    global_col = block_n + warp_n * 32 + col_local
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
+    extra_bias = S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[global_col], S.f32)

-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    for e in S.range(16):
+        global_row = block_m + warp_m * 32 + row_half * 16 + e
+        x = c_lane[e] + bias0
+        x = x / (one + S.exp(-x))
+        x = x + extra_bias
+        Y[global_row, global_col] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_sum = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    shared_var = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
 
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    shared_sum[tid] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = shared_sum[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    d = v - mean
+    shared_var[tid] = d * d
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_var[tid] = shared_var[tid] + shared_var[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    inv_std = S.rsqrt(shared_var[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32) + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+
+
+class ModelNew(nn.Module):

+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    global_col = block_n + warp_n * 32 + col_local
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
+    extra_bias = S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[global_col], S.f32)
     one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

-            x += S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[j], S.f32)

-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    for e in S.range(16):
+        global_row = block_m + warp_m * 32 + row_half * 16 + e
+        x = c_lane[e] + bias0
+        x = x / (one + S.exp(-x))
+        x = x + extra_bias
+        Y[global_row, global_col] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_sum = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    shared_var = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
 
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    shared_sum[tid] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = shared_sum[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    d = v - mean
+    shared_var[tid] = d * d
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_var[tid] = shared_var[tid] + shared_var[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    inv_std = S.rsqrt(shared_var[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32) + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+
+
+class ModelNew(nn.Module):

+BLOCK_M = 64

+BLOCK_K = 16

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32

+

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    global_col = block_n + warp_n * 32 + col_local
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)

+        x = x + extra_bias

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_sum = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    shared_var = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    shared_sum[tid] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = shared_sum[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    d = v - mean
+    shared_var[tid] = d * d
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_var[tid] = shared_var[tid] + shared_var[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(
+        shared_var[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32) + S.convert(EPS, S.f32)
+    )
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+

+BLOCK_M = 64

+BLOCK_K = 16

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    global_col = block_n + warp_n * 32 + col_local
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
+    extra_bias = S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[global_col], S.f32)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_sum = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    shared_var = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    shared_sum[tid] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = shared_sum[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    d = v - mean
+    shared_var[tid] = d * d
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_var[tid] = shared_var[tid] + shared_var[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(
+        shared_var[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32) + S.convert(EPS, S.f32)
+    )
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+        S.syncthreads()
+

+        x = x + extra_bias

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_sum = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    shared_var = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    shared_sum[tid] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_sum[tid] = shared_sum[tid] + shared_sum[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = shared_sum[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    d = v - mean
+    shared_var[tid] = d * d
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 32
+    for _ in S.range(6):
+        if tid < stride:
+            shared_var[tid] = shared_var[tid] + shared_var[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        if stride > 1:
+            stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(
+        shared_var[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32) + S.convert(EPS, S.f32)
+    )
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+
+

codex
The remaining error is small and likely in the group-norm reduction order, not the MFMA tile math. I’m switching that pass to a deterministic per-group accumulation that matches the reference order more closely.
apply patch

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)

-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    global_col = block_n + warp_n * 32 + col_local
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
+    extra_bias = S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[global_col], S.f32)
     one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
-            x = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
-                x += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)

-            x += S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[j], S.f32)

-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):

-            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):

-            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)

+    for e in S.range(16):
+        global_row = block_m + warp_m * 32 + row_half * 16 + e
+        x = c_lane[e] + bias0
+        x = x / (one + S.exp(-x))
+        x = x + extra_bias
+        Y[global_row, global_col] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx

+

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

class Model(nn.Module):
    """
    A model that performs a matrix multiplication, applies Swish activation, sums with a bias term, and normalizes with GroupNorm.
    """
    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, bias_shape):
        super(Model, self).__init__()
        self.matmul = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.bias = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(bias_shape))
        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)

    def forward(self, x):
        """
        Args:
            x (torch.Tensor): Input tensor of shape (batch_size, in_features).
        Returns:
            torch.Tensor: Output tensor of shape (batch_size, out_features).
        """
        x = self.matmul(x)
        x = torch.sigmoid(x) * x  # Swish activation
        x = x + self.bias
        x = self.group_norm(x)
        return x

batch_size = 32768
in_features = 1024
out_features = 4096
num_groups = 64
bias_shape = (out_features,)

def get_inputs():
    return [torch.rand(batch_size, in_features, dtype=torch.bfloat16)]

def get_init_inputs():
    return [in_features, out_features, num_groups, bias_shape]

+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+

+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+

+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]

+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]

+        S.syncthreads()
+

+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)

The sparse checks show the swizzle is behaving for single terms. I’m doing one dense single-`K`-tile check next; if that matches, the remaining gap is just accumulation-order drift against torch’s reference.

def pack(rows):
    x = rows.view(torch.uint16).reshape(64,4).to(torch.int32)
    lo = x[:,0] | (x[:,1] << 16)
    hi = x[:,2] | (x[:,3] << 16)
    return torch.stack([lo,hi], dim=1).to(torch.uint32)

def nz(a_lane,a_pos,b_lane,b_pos):

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()

+    out = d * inv_std

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, sys, torch
path='/workspace/substrate/test/examples/gemm/amdgpu/test_gemm_mfma.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mfma_mod', path)
mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
sys.modules['mfma_mod']=mod
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def pack_rows(x):
    u = x.view(torch.uint16).reshape(64,4).to(torch.int32)
    return torch.stack([u[:,0] | (u[:,1]<<16), u[:,2] | (u[:,3]<<16)], dim=1).to(torch.uint32)

def row_to_lane(row):
    return (row & 3) + (((row >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row >> 4) & 1) * 4)

def pack_A(A):
    frag = torch.zeros((64,4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    for r in range(32):
        lb = row_to_lane(r)
        frag[lb,:] = A[r,:4]
        frag[lb+32,:] = A[r,4:8]
    return pack_rows(frag)

def pack_B(B):
    frag = torch.zeros((64,4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    for c in range(32):
        frag[c,:] = B[:4,c]
        frag[c+32,:] = B[4:8,c]
    return pack_rows(frag)

def decode(Cstor):
    C = torch.zeros((32,32), dtype=torch.float32)
    for lane in range(64):
        row_base = 16 * (lane // 32)
        col = lane % 32
        for e in range(16):
            C[row_base + e, col] = Cstor[lane,e]
    return C

A = torch.randn((32,8), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
B = torch.randn((8,32), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
Cstor = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
mod.gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1,1,1),(64,1,1))](pack_A(A), pack_B(B), Cstor)
C = decode(Cstor.cpu())
ref = A.float().cpu() @ B.float().cpu()
diff = (C-ref).abs()
print('max', diff.max().item(), 'mean', diff.mean().item())
print(diff[:4,:4])

+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

import importlib.util, sys, torch

def load(name, path):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name, path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    sys.modules[name]=mod
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod

+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _group_norm_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_col * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = col_local_load
+            lane_hi = col_local_load + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    global_col = block_n + warp_n * 32 + col_local
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
+    extra_bias = S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[global_col], S.f32)
     one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):

-            x += S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[j], S.f32)

-            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

+        global_row = block_m + warp_m * 32 + row_half * 16 + e
+        x = c_lane[e] + bias0
+        x = x / (one + S.exp(-x))
+        x = x + extra_bias
+        Y[global_row, global_col] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)

+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)

+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31

+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+

+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+

+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+

+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32

+

+            global_col = block_n + col_idx

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]

+

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+

path='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py'

x = torch.zeros((mod.BATCH_SIZE, mod.IN_FEATURES), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
w = torch.zeros((mod.OUT_FEATURES, mod.IN_FEATURES), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
b0 = torch.zeros((mod.OUT_FEATURES,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+

+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+

+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+

+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]

+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31
+            global_col = block_n + col_idx

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]
+        b_packed = b_frag_words[warp_n, lane]

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_idx = tid >> 1
+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx
+            byte_offset = ((global_row * IN_FEATURES) + k_base + k_chunk * 8) * 2
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32
+            word_base = k_chunk * 2
+
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_base, word_base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_frag_words[tile_row, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            col_idx = (tid - 128) >> 1
+            k_chunk = (tid - 128) & 1
+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5
+            col_local_load = col_idx & 31

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_packed = a_frag_words[warp_m, lane]

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
+    extra_bias = S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[global_col], S.f32)

+        x = x + extra_bias
+        Y[global_row, global_col] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid

+        shared_stats[1] = var

+    S.syncthreads()

+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)

codex
I’ve narrowed it to the exact variance path in `GroupNorm`. I’m testing the alternative `E[x^2] - mean^2` formulation against torch’s bf16 `group_norm`; if that’s closer, I’ll switch the kernel to it.
exec
/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import torch
B=64
C=4096
G=64
GS=C//G
EPS=1e-5

torch.manual_seed(0)
y = torch.randn((B, C), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
gw = torch.randn((C,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
gb = torch.randn((C,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
ref = torch.nn.functional.group_norm(y, G, gw, gb, EPS)

# formula 1: serial mean, then sum((x-mean)"'^2)
def gn1(y,gw,gb):
    out = torch.empty_like(y)
    yf = y.float()
    gwf = gw.float(); gbf=gb.float()
    for g in range(G):
        s=slice(g*GS,(g+1)*GS)
        mean = yf[:,s].sum(dim=1, keepdim=True)/GS
        var = ((yf[:,s]-mean)**2).sum(dim=1, keepdim=True)/GS
        out[:,s] = (((yf[:,s]-mean)/torch.sqrt(var+EPS))*gwf[s]+gbf[s]).to(torch.bfloat16)
    return out

# formula 2: sumsq - mean''^2
def gn2(y,gw,gb):
    out = torch.empty_like(y)
    yf = y.float()
    gwf = gw.float(); gbf=gb.float()
    for g in range(G):
        s=slice(g*GS,(g+1)*GS)
        mean = yf[:,s].sum(dim=1, keepdim=True)/GS
        ex2 = (yf[:,s]*yf[:,s]).sum(dim=1, keepdim=True)/GS
        var = ex2 - mean*mean
        out[:,s] = (((yf[:,s]-mean)/torch.sqrt(var+EPS))*gwf[s]+gbf[s]).to(torch.bfloat16)
    return out

for name,fn in [('"'gn1',gn1),('gn2',gn2)]:
    out = fn(y,gw,gb)
    diff=(out-ref).abs().float()
    print(name,diff.max().item(),diff.mean().item())

+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import torch
B=128; C=4096; G=64; GS=C//G; EPS=1e-5
torch.manual_seed(0)
y = torch.randn((B,C), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
gw = torch.randn((C,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
gb = torch.randn((C,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
ref = torch.nn.functional.group_norm(y, G, gw, gb, EPS)

yf=y.float(); gwf=gw.float(); gbf=gb.float(); out=torch.empty_like(y)
for g in range(G):
    s=slice(g*GS,(g+1)*GS)
    vals=yf[:,s]
    mean=torch.zeros((B,1), device='cuda')
    m2=torch.zeros((B,1), device='cuda')
    count=0.0
    for t in range(GS):
        count += 1.0
        x=vals[:,t:t+1]
        delta=x-mean
        mean = mean + delta/count
        delta2=x-mean
        m2 = m2 + delta*delta2
    var = m2/GS
    out[:,s]=(((vals-mean)/torch.sqrt(var+EPS))*gwf[s]+gbf[s]).to(torch.bfloat16)

diff=(out-ref).abs().float(); print(diff.max().item(), diff.mean().item())

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]

+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import torch
B=128; C=4096; G=64; GS=C//G; EPS=1e-5
torch.manual_seed(0)
y = torch.randn((B,C), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
gw = torch.randn((C,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
gb = torch.randn((C,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
ref = torch.nn.functional.group_norm(y, G, gw, gb, EPS)

out=torch.empty_like(y)
for g in range(G):
    s=slice(g*GS,(g+1)*GS)
    vals=y[:,s]
    mean=vals.sum(dim=1, keepdim=True)/GS
    var=((vals-mean)**2).sum(dim=1, keepdim=True)/GS
    out[:,s]=((vals-mean)/torch.sqrt(var+EPS))*gw[s]+gb[s]

diff=(out-ref).abs().float(); print(diff.max().item(), diff.mean().item())

I’m checking which reference path the harness is closer to: a bf16 torch model or a float32 torch model fed with casted inputs. That determines whether I should preserve bf16 rounding or keep more of the epilogue in f32.

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, sys, torch

def load(name, path):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name, path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    sys.modules[name]=mod
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod

cand = load('cand_out','/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py')
refm = load('refm2','/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/input_model.py')

torch.manual_seed(0)
base = refm.Model(*refm.get_init_inputs()).cuda()
model = cand.ModelNew(*refm.get_init_inputs()).cuda()
model.load_state_dict(base.state_dict())
x_bf16 = refm.get_inputs()[0].cuda()
with torch.no_grad():
    y_model = model(x_bf16)

    ref_bf16 = refm.Model(*refm.get_init_inputs()).cuda().to(torch.bfloat16)
    ref_bf16.load_state_dict({k:v.to(torch.bfloat16) for k,v in base.state_dict().items()})
    y_bf16 = ref_bf16(x_bf16)
    d1 = (y_model - y_bf16).abs().float()
    print('vs bf16 ref', d1.max().item(), d1.mean().item())

    x_f32 = x_bf16.float()
    y_f32 = base(x_f32).to(torch.bfloat16)
    d2 = (y_model - y_f32).abs().float()

+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31
+
+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
