+            k_chunk = tid & 1
+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+

+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32

+

+            tile_col = col_idx >> 5

+

+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_frag_words[tile_col, lane_hi, word_base + 1] = packed[3]

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)

import importlib.util, sys, torch

def load(name, path):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name, path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    sys.modules[name]=mod
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod

cand = load('cand_out','/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py')
refm = load('refm2','/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/input_model.py')

x = refm.get_inputs()[0].cuda()
with torch.no_grad():
    y = torch.empty((cand.BATCH_SIZE, cand.OUT_FEATURES), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    cand.gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel[cand._gemm_launch](x, base.matmul.weight.contiguous(), base.matmul.bias.contiguous(), base.bias.contiguous(), y)
    y2 = torch.nn.functional.group_norm(y, cand.NUM_GROUPS, base.group_norm.weight.contiguous(), base.group_norm.bias.contiguous(), cand.EPS)
    yref = base(x)
    diff=(y2-yref).abs().float()
    print(diff.max().item(), diff.mean().item())

+def gemm_bias_silu_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    wave = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_m = wave >> 1
+    warp_n = wave & 1
+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31

+    a_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, OUT_FEATURES * IN_FEATURES * 2)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

+            tile_row = row_idx >> 5
+            row_local = row_idx & 31
+            global_row = block_m + row_idx

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+
+            lane_base = (row_local & 3) + (((row_local >> 2) & 3) * 8) + (((row_local >> 4) & 1) * 4)
+            lane_hi = lane_base + 32

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+

def load(name, path):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name, path)

+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)

import importlib.util, sys, torch

def load(name, path):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name, path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    sys.modules[name]=mod
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod

+    lane = tid & 63

+    row_half = lane >> 5
+    col_local = lane & 31

Implemented an MFMA-based Substrate path in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py) with:
- `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32`
- `S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4`
- LDS staging
- a 4-wave `2 x 2` wave grid for the GEMM tile
- a separate Substrate group-norm pass

I ran the required harness command and wrote results to [debug_eval.jsonl](/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p37/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/debug_eval.jsonl). The kernel compiles and runs, but it does not pass correctness yet: `max_difference=0.03125`, `avg_difference=0.001465`, `correctness=false`.

I did not modify `candidate_input.py`.

+@substrate.jit
+def group_norm_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    col = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+
+    shared_stats = S.make_shared((2,), S.f32)
+
+    if tid == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean = mean + S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d_ref = S.convert(Y[row, group * GROUP_SIZE + t], S.f32) - mean
+            var = var + d_ref * d_ref
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_stats[0] = mean
+        shared_stats[1] = var
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    v = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
+    d = v - shared_stats[0]
+    inv_std = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(shared_stats[1] + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+    out = d * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+    Y[row, col] = S.convert(out, S.bf16)
+
